from ultralytics import YOLO
model = YOLO("yolo11n.pt")

model.train(
    data="/kaggle/working/ffb_localization_depth.yaml",
    epochs=50,
    imgsz=640,
    batch=16,
    device="cuda",
    seed=42,
    project="/kaggle/working/runs/detect",
    name="exp_a2_depth_seed42",
)
